Note: To make it fit in paste, I cut out some likely useless functions 'aCredxxx /aCrd' offset 000F21C (aCred716) to 000104D0 (aCred000) and more, which is noted at those positions
like 'HERE's a GAP' > details/offset to offset. ONLY STUFF THAT LOOKED UNIMPORTANT/GENERIC or likely known in other SA research, I removed (very selectively).

Details on this file: 

This is PC offset map/research!

Origin is mobile SA, but my reversal is aimed at PC now, methods;
Mostly autogenerated from the android SA stuff,

Built a script which analyzed calls-from and calls-to and named functions according to that

basically if a function is only called from one place in android, I assume it's also only called from the same place on PC

-> we have a name for the caller

Knowing this, you can imagine to which degree you can rely on this research/reversal. not perfect sadly due to compiler differences.
Took some precautions to ensure accuracy though, no rendering or init stuff as that differs a lot between pc and android (opengl vs directx)
